clickables:['||What do I need to bring when picking up the car?|class=android.view.View|parent=android.widget.ScrollView|index=0', "||When picking up your car, you'll need:|class=android.view.View|parent=android.view.View|index=0", "||1.\nDriver's license: The main driver's license needs to have been held for at least 1 or 2 years (depending on the rental company's policy). Additional drivers must also present their driver's license. If your driver's license is not written using English characters (e.g. Arabic, Greek, Chinese, etc.), you must bring an international driving permit along with your original license. Specific requirements may differ depending on the rental supplier.
